###  Helminauha‚ÇÅ

* _This rare proper noun overlaps more common *Helminauha* (pearls)_
* UPOS:  PROPN
* in KOTUS dictionary under:  9
* Origins: finer 
* Possible NER class:  CULTGRP
* Blacklisted:  PROPN-BLOCKING
